
#include "GeneralTools.h"
#include "TMinuit.h"
#include "../include/setuputil.hpp"
#include "../include/Inputs.hpp"

using namespace std;
using namespace CP_analysis;

void Asym_Calc();

extern void fcnk0(Int_t & npar, double *gin, double &f, double *x, Int_t iflag);

double LogPoissonProb(double Nobserved, double Nexpected);

string _name;

//double Asym = 0.040;

Int_t _nparam;

ofstream fout;

int main(int argc, char *argv[])
{

   TEnv *TheSettings;
   std::vector<std::string> parameterfiles;
   char *ConfigFile;

   string _channel;
   string observable;
   string _sys_name;
   string _out_file_name;
   string _output_dir;

   for (int h=1;h < argc;h++)
   {
      char *argch = argv[h];

      if(strcmp(argch,"-all")==0)
      {
         setuputil::CHANNEL_TYPE = 0;
         _channel = "ljets";
         cout << "Running for combination of all channels" << endl;
      }

      if(strcmp(argch,"-e")==0)
      {
         setuputil::CHANNEL_TYPE = 1;
         _channel = "ejets";
         cout << "Running for only e+jets channel" << endl;
      }

      if(strcmp(argch,"-mu")==0)
      {
         setuputil::CHANNEL_TYPE = 2;
         _channel = "mujets";
         cout << "Running for only mu+jets channel" << endl;
      }

      if(strcmp(argch,"-sys")==0)
      {
         _sys_name = argv[h+1];
         h = h+1;
      }

      if(strcmp(argch,"-outdir")==0)
      {
         _output_dir = argv[h+1];
         h = h+1;
      }
   }
   
   //read argument
   for (int i=1;i < argc;i++)
   {  
      char *argchar = argv[i];

      if(strcmp(argchar,"O1")==0)
      {
         setuputil::Observable = 1;
         observable = argchar;
         _out_file_name = _output_dir+"/"+_channel+"_"+observable+"_"+_sys_name+".txt";          
         fout.open(_out_file_name.c_str());
         cout << "Asymmetry for O1 will be calculated!" << endl;
      }

      if(strcmp(argchar,"O2")==0)
      {
         setuputil::Observable = 2;
         observable = argchar;
         _out_file_name = _output_dir+"/"+_channel+"_"+observable+"_"+_sys_name+".txt";
         fout.open(_out_file_name.c_str());
         cout << "Asymmetry for O2 will be calculated!" << endl;
      }

      if(strcmp(argchar,"O3")==0)
      {
         setuputil::Observable = 3;
         observable = argchar;
         _out_file_name = _output_dir+"/"+_channel+"_"+observable+"_"+_sys_name+".txt";
         fout.open(_out_file_name.c_str());
         cout << "Asymmetry for O3 will be calculated!" << endl;
      }

      if(strcmp(argchar,"O4")==0)
      {
         setuputil::Observable = 4;
         observable = argchar;
         _out_file_name = _output_dir+"/"+_channel+"_"+observable+"_"+_sys_name+".txt";
         fout.open(_out_file_name.c_str());
         cout << "Asymmetry for O4 will be calculated!" << endl;
      }

      if(strcmp(argchar,"O7")==0)
      {
         setuputil::Observable = 7;
         observable = argchar;
         _out_file_name = _output_dir+"/"+_channel+"_"+observable+"_"+_sys_name+".txt";
         fout.open(_out_file_name.c_str());
         cout << "Asymmetry for O7 will be calculated!" << endl;
      }

      if(strcmp(argchar,"Oa")==0)
      {
         setuputil::Observable = 61;
         observable = argchar;
         _out_file_name = _output_dir+"/"+_channel+"_"+observable+"_"+_sys_name+".txt";
         fout.open(_out_file_name.c_str());
         cout << "Asymmetry for Oa will be calculated!" << endl;
      }

      if(strcmp(argchar,"Ob")==0)
      {
         setuputil::Observable = 62;
         observable = argchar;
         _out_file_name = _output_dir+"/"+_channel+"_"+observable+"_"+_sys_name+".txt";
         fout.open(_out_file_name.c_str());
         cout << "Asymmetry for Ob will be calculated!" << endl;
      }

      if(strcmp(argchar, "-config")==0)
      {
         for (int j=1;j<=3;j++)
         {
            ConfigFile=argv[i+j];
            parameterfiles.push_back(ConfigFile);
         }
         //++i;
         i=i+3;

         for (unsigned int par=0;par<parameterfiles.size();par++)
         {
            cout << "Use parameter file " << parameterfiles[par] << endl;
         }
         //cout << "Use parameter file " << ConfigFile << endl;
      }
     
      if(strcmp(argchar,"-help")==0)
      {
         cout << endl << endl << endl;
         cout << "Options for Asymmetry calculation code: " << endl;
         cout << "--------------------------------------- "  << endl << endl; 
         cout << " Physics Observables O1, O2, O3, O4, O7, Oa, Ob"  << endl; 
         cout << " -all ............ e+4jets and mu+4jets - default " << endl;
         cout << " -e   ............ only e+4jets " << endl;
         cout << " -mu  ............ only mu+4jets " << endl;
         cout << " -config     to set the config for general settings and parameters. THIS HAS TO BE SPECIFIED FOR MEANINGFUL RESULTS!" << endl;
         return 0;
      }
   }//end of loop of argument
   cout << endl << endl << endl;

   TheSettings=new TEnv("Settings");  
   read_my_params *setmyparameters=new read_my_params(TheSettings, parameterfiles);
   std::string directory = ".";
   setmyparameters->SetupFile(directory); 
   if(!(setmyparameters->GotOne()))
   {
      std::cout<<"ATTENTION! NO PARAMETER FILE FOUND FOR SETTING THE PARAMETERS!"<<std::endl;

   Double_t eps_sig_e = TheSettings->GetValue("eps_sig_e",0.);
   Double_t eps_sig_e_err = TheSettings->GetValue("eps_sig_e_err",0.);
   Double_t eps_sig_mu = TheSettings->GetValue("eps_sig_mu",0.);
   Double_t eps_sig_mu_err = TheSettings->GetValue("eps_sig_mu_err",0.);
   Double_t eps_qcd_e = TheSettings->GetValue("eps_qcd_e",0.);
   Double_t eps_qcd_e_err = TheSettings->GetValue("eps_qcd_e_err",0.);
   Double_t eps_qcd_mu = TheSettings->GetValue("eps_qcd_mu",0.);
   Double_t eps_qcd_mu_err = TheSettings->GetValue("eps_qcd_mu_err",0.);

   Double_t ejets_N_LT_obs = TheSettings->GetValue("ejets_N_LT",0.);
   Double_t mujets_N_LT_obs = TheSettings->GetValue("mujets_N_LT",0.);
  
   Inputs::Selection_eff_e = TheSettings->GetValue("Selection_Eff_e", 0.);
   Inputs::Selection_eff_mu = TheSettings->GetValue("Selection_Eff_mu", 0.);

   Inputs::Inputs::Luminosity = TheSettings->GetValue("Luminosity", 4281.66);
   Inputs::Br_tt_ej = TheSettings->GetValue("Br_ttbar_ej", 0.1721);
   Inputs::Br_tt_mj = TheSettings->GetValue("Br_ttbar_mj", 0.17137);

   Inputs::N_param = TheSettings->GetValue("N_parameters", 100);
   Inputs::Step_Size = TheSettings->GetValue("Step_Size", 0.0001);
   Inputs::SET_ERR = TheSettings->GetValue("SET_ERR", 0.5);

   //cout << mujets_hOb_4ttll_fminus << "  " << ejets_hOb_4ttll_asym << " " << eps_sig_mu << endl;
   Inputs::eps_sig_e = eps_sig_e;
   Inputs::eps_sig_e_err = eps_sig_e_err;
   Inputs::eps_sig_mu = eps_sig_mu;
   Inputs::eps_sig_mu_err = eps_sig_mu_err;
   Inputs::eps_qcd_e = eps_qcd_e;
   Inputs::eps_qcd_e_err = eps_qcd_e_err;
   Inputs::eps_qcd_mu = eps_qcd_mu;
   Inputs::eps_qcd_mu_err = eps_qcd_mu_err;

   Inputs::c_e = Inputs::eps_qcd_e*(1-Inputs::eps_sig_e)/((1-Inputs::eps_qcd_e)*Inputs::eps_sig_e);
   Inputs::c_mu = Inputs::eps_qcd_mu*(1-Inputs::eps_sig_mu)/((1-Inputs::eps_qcd_mu)*Inputs::eps_sig_mu);

   Inputs::N_LT_obs_e = ejets_N_LT_obs;
   Inputs::N_LT_obs_mu = mujets_N_LT_obs;


   if (setuputil::Observable == 0)
   {
      cout << "You have to specify a physics observable name to calculate like O1, O2, O3 and so on!!!" << endl;
      return 0;
   }

   if (setuputil::Observable == 1)
   {
      //e+jets
      Inputs::N_w_e = 0;
      Inputs::f_w_p_e = 0;
      Inputs::f_w_m_e = 0;
      Inputs::N_ttbar_e = 0;
      Inputs::N_mc_e = 0;
      Inputs::f_mc_p_e = 0;
      Inputs::f_mc_m_e = 0;
      Inputs::N_qcd_e = 0;
      Inputs::f_qcd_p_e = 0;
      Inputs::f_qcd_m_e = 0;
      Inputs::N_plus_obs_e = 0;
      Inputs::N_minus_obs_e = 0;

      Inputs::N_w_e = ejets_hO1_4WJet0_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4WJet0_Nminus + ejets_hO1_4WJetB_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4WJetB_Nminus 
                      + ejets_hO1_4WJetC_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4WJetC_Nminus + ejets_hO1_4WJetC1_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4WJetC1_Nminus;
      Inputs::f_w_p_e = (ejets_hO1_4WJet0_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4WJetB_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4WJetC_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4WJetC1_Nplus)/Inputs::N_w_e;
      if (Inputs::f_w_p_e == 0){Inputs::f_w_m_e = 0;} 
      else {Inputs::f_w_m_e = 1 - Inputs::f_w_p_e;}

      Inputs::N_ttbar_e = ejets_hO1_4TTbar_plus_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4TTbar_plus_Nminus;

      Inputs::N_mc_e = ejets_hO1_4ZbbEE_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4ZbbEE_Nminus + ejets_hO1_4ZbbTauTau_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4ZbbTauTau_Nminus + 
                       ejets_hO1_4ZccEE_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4ZccEE_Nminus + ejets_hO1_4ZccTauTau_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4ZccTauTau_Nminus +
                       ejets_hO1_4ZlpEE_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4ZlpEE_Nminus + ejets_hO1_4ZlpTauTau_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4ZlpTauTau_Nminus +
                       ejets_hO1_4tb_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4tb_Nminus + ejets_hO1_4tbq_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4tbq_Nminus +
                       ejets_hO1_4WW_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4WW_Nminus +
                       ejets_hO1_4WZ_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4WZ_Nminus +
                       ejets_hO1_4ZZ_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4ZZ_Nminus +
                       ejets_hO1_4ttll_Nplus + ejets_hO1_4ttll_Nminus;

      Inputs::N_w_mu = mujets_hOa_4WJet0_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4WJet0_Nminus + mujets_hOa_4WJetB_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4WJetB_Nminus
                      + mujets_hOa_4WJetC_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4WJetC_Nminus + mujets_hOa_4WJetC1_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4WJetC1_Nminus;
      Inputs::f_w_p_mu = (mujets_hOa_4WJet0_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4WJetB_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4WJetC_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4WJetC1_Nplus)/Inputs::N_w_mu;
      if (Inputs::f_w_p_mu == 0){Inputs::f_w_m_mu = 0;}
      else {Inputs::f_w_m_mu = 1 - Inputs::f_w_p_mu;}

      Inputs::N_ttbar_mu = mujets_hOa_4TTbar_plus_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4TTbar_plus_Nminus;

      Inputs::N_mc_mu = mujets_hOa_4ZbbMuMu_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4ZbbMuMu_Nminus + mujets_hOa_4ZbbTauTau_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4ZbbTauTau_Nminus +
                        mujets_hOa_4ZccMuMu_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4ZccMuMu_Nminus + mujets_hOa_4ZccTauTau_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4ZccTauTau_Nminus +
                        mujets_hOa_4ZlpMuMu_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4ZlpMuMu_Nminus + mujets_hOa_4ZlpTauTau_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4ZlpTauTau_Nminus +
                        mujets_hOa_4tb_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4tb_Nminus + mujets_hOa_4tbq_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4tbq_Nminus +
                        mujets_hOa_4WW_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4WW_Nminus +
                        mujets_hOa_4WZ_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4WZ_Nminus +
                        mujets_hOa_4ZZ_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4ZZ_Nminus +
                        mujets_hOa_4ttll_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4ttll_Nminus;
      Inputs::f_mc_p_mu = (mujets_hOa_4ZbbMuMu_Nplus+mujets_hOa_4ZbbTauTau_Nplus+mujets_hOa_4ZccMuMu_Nplus+mujets_hOa_4ZccTauTau_Nplus
                           +mujets_hOa_4ZlpMuMu_Nplus+mujets_hOa_4ZlpTauTau_Nplus+mujets_hOa_4tb_Nplus+mujets_hOa_4tbq_Nplus
                           +mujets_hOa_4WW_Nplus+mujets_hOa_4WZ_Nplus+mujets_hOa_4ZZ_Nplus+mujets_hOa_4ttll_Nplus)/Inputs::N_mc_mu;
      if (Inputs::f_mc_p_mu == 0){Inputs::f_mc_m_mu = 0;}
      else {Inputs::f_mc_m_mu = 1 - Inputs::f_mc_p_mu;}

      Inputs::N_qcd_mu = mujets_hOa_4QCD_Nplus + mujets_hOa_4QCD_Nminus;
      Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu = mujets_hOa_4QCD_fplus;
      if (Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu == 0){Inputs::f_qcd_m_mu = 0;}
      else {Inputs::f_qcd_m_mu = 1 - Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu;}

      Inputs::N_plus_obs_mu = mujets_hOa_4Data_Nplus;

      Inputs::N_minus_obs_mu = mujets_hOa_4Data_Nminus;

      if (setuputil::CHANNEL_TYPE == 0)
      {
         Inputs::Init_Asym = (ejets_hOa_4TTbar_plus_asym + mujets_hOa_4TTbar_plus_asym)/2;
         Inputs::Init_Asym_err = (ejets_hOa_4TTbar_plus_asym_err + mujets_hOa_4TTbar_plus_asym_err)/2;
      }
      else if (setuputil::CHANNEL_TYPE == 1)
      {
         Inputs::Init_Asym = ejets_hOa_4TTbar_plus_asym;
         Inputs::Init_Asym_err = ejets_hOa_4TTbar_plus_asym_err;
      }
      else if (setuputil::CHANNEL_TYPE == 2)
      {
         Inputs::Init_Asym = mujets_hOa_4TTbar_plus_asym;
         Inputs::Init_Asym_err = mujets_hOa_4TTbar_plus_asym_err;
      }
   }

   if (setuputil::Observable == 62)
   {
      //e+jets
      Inputs::N_w_e = 0;
      Inputs::f_w_p_e = 0;
      Inputs::f_w_m_e = 0;
      Inputs::N_ttbar_e = 0;
      Inputs::N_mc_e = 0;
      Inputs::f_mc_p_e = 0;
      Inputs::f_mc_m_e = 0;
      Inputs::N_qcd_e = 0;
      Inputs::f_qcd_p_e = 0;
      Inputs::f_qcd_m_e = 0;   
      Inputs::N_plus_obs_e = 0;
      Inputs::N_minus_obs_e = 0;

      Inputs::N_w_e = ejets_hOb_4WJet0_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4WJet0_Nminus + ejets_hOb_4WJetB_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4WJetB_Nminus
                      + ejets_hOb_4WJetC_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4WJetC_Nminus + ejets_hOb_4WJetC1_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4WJetC1_Nminus;
      Inputs::f_w_p_e = (ejets_hOb_4WJet0_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4WJetB_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4WJetC_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4WJetC1_Nplus)/Inputs::N_w_e;
      if (Inputs::f_w_p_e == 0){Inputs::f_w_m_e = 0;}
      else {Inputs::f_w_m_e = 1 - Inputs::f_w_p_e;}

      Inputs::N_ttbar_e = ejets_hOb_4TTbar_plus_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4TTbar_plus_Nminus;

      Inputs::N_mc_e = ejets_hOb_4ZbbEE_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4ZbbEE_Nminus + ejets_hOb_4ZbbTauTau_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4ZbbTauTau_Nminus +
                       ejets_hOb_4ZccEE_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4ZccEE_Nminus + ejets_hOb_4ZccTauTau_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4ZccTauTau_Nminus +
                       ejets_hOb_4ZlpEE_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4ZlpEE_Nminus + ejets_hOb_4ZlpTauTau_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4ZlpTauTau_Nminus +
                       ejets_hOb_4tb_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4tb_Nminus + ejets_hOb_4tbq_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4tbq_Nminus +
                       ejets_hOb_4WW_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4WW_Nminus +
                       ejets_hOb_4WZ_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4WZ_Nminus +
                       ejets_hOb_4ZZ_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4ZZ_Nminus +
                       ejets_hOb_4ttll_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4ttll_Nminus;
      Inputs::f_mc_p_e = (ejets_hOb_4ZbbEE_Nplus+ejets_hOb_4ZbbTauTau_Nplus+ejets_hOb_4ZccEE_Nplus+ejets_hOb_4ZccTauTau_Nplus+ejets_hOb_4ZlpEE_Nplus+ejets_hOb_4ZlpTauTau_Nplus
                          +ejets_hOb_4tb_Nplus+ejets_hOb_4tbq_Nplus+ejets_hOb_4WW_Nplus+ejets_hOb_4WZ_Nplus+ejets_hOb_4ZZ_Nplus+ejets_hOb_4ttll_Nplus)/Inputs::N_mc_e;
      if (Inputs::f_mc_p_e == 0){Inputs::f_mc_m_e = 0;}
      else {Inputs::f_mc_m_e = 1 - Inputs::f_mc_p_e;}
      cout << Inputs::N_w_e << " " << Inputs::f_w_p_e << " " << Inputs::N_mc_e << " " << Inputs::f_mc_p_e << endl;
      Inputs::N_qcd_e = ejets_hOb_4QCD_Nplus + ejets_hOb_4QCD_Nminus;
      Inputs::f_qcd_p_e = ejets_hOb_4QCD_fplus;
      if (Inputs::f_qcd_p_e == 0){Inputs::f_qcd_m_e = 0;}
      else {Inputs::f_qcd_m_e = 1 - Inputs::f_qcd_p_e;}

      Inputs::N_plus_obs_e = ejets_hOb_4Data_Nplus;

      Inputs::N_minus_obs_e = ejets_hOb_4Data_Nminus;

      //mu+jets
      Inputs::N_w_mu = 0;
      Inputs::f_w_p_mu = 0;
      Inputs::f_w_m_mu = 0;
      Inputs::N_ttbar_mu = 0;
      Inputs::N_mc_mu = 0;
      Inputs::f_mc_p_mu = 0;
      Inputs::f_mc_m_mu = 0;
      Inputs::N_qcd_mu = 0;
      Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu = 0;
      Inputs::f_qcd_m_mu = 0;
      Inputs::N_plus_obs_mu = 0;
      Inputs::N_minus_obs_mu = 0;

      Inputs::N_w_mu = mujets_hOb_4WJet0_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4WJet0_Nminus + mujets_hOb_4WJetB_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4WJetB_Nminus
                      + mujets_hOb_4WJetC_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4WJetC_Nminus + mujets_hOb_4WJetC1_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4WJetC1_Nminus;
      Inputs::f_w_p_mu = (mujets_hOb_4WJet0_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4WJetB_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4WJetC_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4WJetC1_Nplus)/Inputs::N_w_mu;
      if (Inputs::f_w_p_mu == 0){Inputs::f_w_m_mu = 0;}
      else {Inputs::f_w_m_mu = 1 - Inputs::f_w_p_mu;}

      Inputs::N_ttbar_mu = mujets_hOb_4TTbar_plus_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4TTbar_plus_Nminus;

      Inputs::N_mc_mu = mujets_hOb_4ZbbMuMu_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4ZbbMuMu_Nminus + mujets_hOb_4ZbbTauTau_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4ZbbTauTau_Nminus +
                        mujets_hOb_4ZccMuMu_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4ZccMuMu_Nminus + mujets_hOb_4ZccTauTau_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4ZccTauTau_Nminus +
                        mujets_hOb_4ZlpMuMu_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4ZlpMuMu_Nminus + mujets_hOb_4ZlpTauTau_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4ZlpTauTau_Nminus +
                        mujets_hOb_4tb_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4tb_Nminus + mujets_hOb_4tbq_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4tbq_Nminus +
                        mujets_hOb_4WW_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4WW_Nminus +
                        mujets_hOb_4WZ_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4WZ_Nminus +
                        mujets_hOb_4ZZ_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4ZZ_Nminus +
                        mujets_hOb_4ttll_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4ttll_Nminus;
      Inputs::f_mc_p_mu = (mujets_hOb_4ZbbMuMu_Nplus+mujets_hOb_4ZbbTauTau_Nplus+mujets_hOb_4ZccMuMu_Nplus+mujets_hOb_4ZccTauTau_Nplus
                           +mujets_hOb_4ZlpMuMu_Nplus+mujets_hOb_4ZlpTauTau_Nplus+mujets_hOb_4tb_Nplus+mujets_hOb_4tbq_Nplus
                           +mujets_hOb_4WW_Nplus+mujets_hOb_4WZ_Nplus+mujets_hOb_4ZZ_Nplus+mujets_hOb_4ttll_Nplus)/Inputs::N_mc_mu;
      if (Inputs::f_mc_p_mu == 0){Inputs::f_mc_m_mu = 0;}
      else {Inputs::f_mc_m_mu = 1 - Inputs::f_mc_p_mu;}

      Inputs::N_qcd_mu = mujets_hOb_4QCD_Nplus + mujets_hOb_4QCD_Nminus;
      Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu = mujets_hOb_4QCD_fplus;
      if (Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu == 0){Inputs::f_qcd_m_mu = 0;}
      else {Inputs::f_qcd_m_mu = 1 - Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu;}

      Inputs::N_plus_obs_mu = mujets_hOb_4Data_Nplus;

      Inputs::N_minus_obs_mu = mujets_hOb_4Data_Nminus;

      if (setuputil::CHANNEL_TYPE == 0)
      {
         Inputs::Init_Asym = (ejets_hOb_4TTbar_plus_asym + mujets_hOb_4TTbar_plus_asym)/2;
         Inputs::Init_Asym_err = (ejets_hOb_4TTbar_plus_asym_err + mujets_hOb_4TTbar_plus_asym_err)/2;
      }
      else if (setuputil::CHANNEL_TYPE == 1)
      {
         Inputs::Init_Asym = ejets_hOb_4TTbar_plus_asym;
         Inputs::Init_Asym_err = ejets_hOb_4TTbar_plus_asym_err;
      }
      else if (setuputil::CHANNEL_TYPE == 2)
      {
         Inputs::Init_Asym = mujets_hOb_4TTbar_plus_asym;
         Inputs::Init_Asym_err = mujets_hOb_4TTbar_plus_asym_err;
      }
   }

   //run asymmetry fitting
   Asym_Calc();

}//end of main function


void Asym_Calc() 
{
   _nparam = Inputs::N_param;
   double x[_nparam];
   double x_err[_nparam];
   double step_size = Inputs::Step_Size;
   x[_nparam-1] = Inputs::Init_Asym; 
   x[_nparam-2] = 8.13; 
   //cout << "x[_nparam-1]" << x[_nparam-1] << endl;
  
    TMinuit *gMinuit = new TMinuit(_nparam);
  
    Int_t ierflg = 0;
    static Double_t migradPar[2] ={10000000,.001}; // Migrad parameters
    static Double_t minosPar=0; // minos parameter
    static Double_t UP[1] = {Inputs::SET_ERR};
    static Double_t p0=1;
    static Double_t p1=1;
    static Double_t rnd_seed[1]={123456789};

    gMinuit->mninit(5,6,7);
    gMinuit->SetFCN(fcnk0);

    //gMinuit->mnparm(_nparam-3, "L-T",Inputs::N_LT_obs_e, 0.01, 0, 0, ierflg);
    //gMinuit->mnparm(_nparam-2, "Asymmetry_ww", -Inputs::Init_Asym, step_size, 0, 0, ierflg);
    //gMinuit->mnparm(_nparam-1, "Asymmetry_cw", Inputs::Init_Asym, step_size, 0, 0, ierflg); 
    gMinuit->mnparm(_nparam-2, "sigma_tt",8.13, step_size, 0, 0, ierflg);
    gMinuit->mnparm(_nparam-1, "Asymmetry", Inputs::Init_Asym, step_size, 0, 0, ierflg); 
  
    for( int i = 0; i < _nparam; i++ ) gMinuit->FixParameter(i);
    for( int ipar = 1; ipar < _nparam; ipar++ ) 
    {
    //   if (ipar == 2) continue;
       gMinuit->Release(_nparam - ipar);
    }
    gMinuit->mnexcm("CALL FCN", &p1 ,1,ierflg);
    gMinuit->mnexcm("SET PRINT", &p0 ,0,ierflg);
    gMinuit->mnexcm("SET RAN", rnd_seed ,1,ierflg);
    gMinuit->mnexcm("MIGRAD", migradPar ,2,ierflg);
    for( int i = 0; i < _nparam; i++ ) gMinuit->GetParameter(i, x[i], x_err[i]);
    //UP=1 for chi-square, UP=0.5 for negative log likelihood
    gMinuit->mnexcm("SET ERR",UP,1,ierflg);
    gMinuit->mnexcm("MINOS", &minosPar, 0, ierflg);
    //gMinuit->mnexcm("SCAN", p2, 1, ierflg);

    //double asym_cw, errplus_cw, errminus_cw, errparab_cw, gcc_cw, dummy_cw;
    //double asym_ww, errplus_ww, errminus_ww, errparab_ww, gcc_ww, dummy_ww;
    double asym, errplus, errminus, errparab, gcc, dummy;
    double xstt, xstt_errplus, xstt_errminus, xstt_errparab, xstt_gcc, xstt_dummy;
    int istat, nparx, npari;
    double fmin, fedm, errdef;
    gMinuit->mnstat(fmin,fedm,errdef,npari,nparx,istat);
    gMinuit->GetParameter(_nparam-1, asym, dummy);
    gMinuit->mnerrs(_nparam-1, errplus, errminus, errparab, gcc);
    gMinuit->GetParameter(_nparam-2, xstt, xstt_dummy);
    gMinuit->mnerrs(_nparam-2, xstt_errplus, xstt_errminus, xstt_errparab, xstt_gcc);
/*  //true asym and dilution
    gMinuit->GetParameter(_nparam-2, asym_ww, dummy_ww);
    gMinuit->GetParameter(_nparam-1, asym_cw, dummy_cw);
    gMinuit->mnerrs(_nparam-2, errplus_ww, errminus_ww, errparab_ww, gcc_ww);
    gMinuit->mnerrs(_nparam-1, errplus_cw, errminus_cw, errparab_cw, gcc_cw);
*/
/*    
    fout << asym_cw << " " << errplus_cw << " " << errminus_cw << endl;
    fout << asym_ww << " " << errplus_ww << " " << errminus_ww << endl;
*/
    fout << asym << " " << errplus << " " << errminus << endl;
    fout.close();
    //cout << 0.915*asym_cw + 0.085*asym_ww << " " << sqrt((0.915*errplus_cw)*(0.915*errplus_cw)+(0.085*errminus_cw)*(0.085*errminus_ww)) << endl;
    cout << endl << endl;
    cout << "========================================================================================================= " << endl;
    cout << "====                             Summary of likelihood fit by Minuit                                ===== " << endl;
    cout << "========================================================================================================= " << endl;
    cout << endl << endl;
    printf("----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n");
    cout << "Asymmetry O" << setuputil::Observable << " = " << asym << " +" << errplus << " -" << errminus << "  (MINOS errors)" << endl;
    cout << "xsection ttbar O" << setuputil::Observable << " = " << xstt << " +" << xstt_errplus << " -" << xstt_errminus << "  (MINOS errors)" << endl;
    printf("----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n");
    cout << endl << endl << endl;
}



//============================================================================
//===
//===
//===
//===                     Likelihood function 
//===
//===
//===
//============================================================================

//npar: number of free parameters involved in minimization
//gin: computed gradient values (optional)
//f: the function value itself
//x: vector of constant and variable parameters
//flag: to switch between several actions of FCN
//============================================================================
void fcnk0(Int_t & npar, double *gin, double &f, double *x, Int_t iflag)
//============================================================================
{

   double loglhood = 0;
   Double_t f_cw_e = 0.92;
   Double_t f_ww_e = 0.08;
   Double_t f_cw_mu = 0.94;
   Double_t f_ww_mu = 0.06;
   Double_t N_plus_pred_e, N_minus_pred_e, N_LT_pred_e;
   Double_t N_plus_pred_mu, N_minus_pred_mu, N_LT_pred_mu;
   Double_t N_pre_tt_e; 
   Double_t N_pre_tt_mu; 
   //cout << N_pre_tt << " " << Inputs::N_ttbar_e << " " << x[_nparam-2] << endl;
   //N_pre_tt_e = Inputs::Luminosity * Inputs::Br_tt_ej * Inputs::Selection_eff_e * x[_nparam-2];
   //N_pre_tt_mu = Inputs::Luminosity * Inputs::Br_tt_mj * Inputs::Selection_eff_mu * x[_nparam-2];

   if (setuputil::CHANNEL_TYPE == 0)
   {
 /*   ///test
      N_plus_pred_e = Inputs::N_ttbar_e * (1-Inputs::c_e) * (1 + x[_nparam-1])/2 + 
                      (Inputs::N_w_e*Inputs::f_w_p_e + Inputs::N_mc_e * Inputs::f_mc_p_e) * (1-Inputs::c_e) + 
                      (Inputs::N_qcd_e + Inputs::c_e * (Inputs::N_ttbar_e + Inputs::N_w_e + Inputs::N_mc_e))*Inputs::f_qcd_p_e;
      N_minus_pred_e = Inputs::N_ttbar_e * (1-Inputs::c_e) * (1 - x[_nparam-1])/2 + 
                       (Inputs::N_w_e*(1-Inputs::f_w_p_e) + Inputs::N_mc_e * (1-Inputs::f_mc_p_e)) * (1-Inputs::c_e) + 
                       (Inputs::N_qcd_e + Inputs::c_e * (Inputs::N_ttbar_e + Inputs::N_w_e + Inputs::N_mc_e))*(1-Inputs::f_qcd_p_e);
      N_LT_pred_e = (1-Inputs::eps_sig_e)*(Inputs::N_ttbar_e + Inputs::N_w_e + Inputs::N_mc_e)/Inputs::eps_sig_e 
                    + (1-Inputs::eps_qcd_e)*Inputs::N_qcd_e/Inputs::eps_qcd_e;

      N_plus_pred_mu = Inputs::N_ttbar_mu * (1-Inputs::c_mu) * (1 + x[_nparam-1])/2 + 
                       (Inputs::N_w_mu*Inputs::f_w_p_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu * Inputs::f_mc_p_mu) * (1-Inputs::c_mu) + 
                       (Inputs::N_qcd_mu + Inputs::c_mu * (Inputs::N_ttbar_mu + Inputs::N_w_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu))*Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu;
      N_minus_pred_mu = Inputs::N_ttbar_mu * (1-Inputs::c_mu) * (1 - x[_nparam-1])/2 + 
                        (Inputs::N_w_mu*(1-Inputs::f_w_p_mu) + Inputs::N_mc_mu * (1-Inputs::f_mc_p_mu)) * (1-Inputs::c_mu) +
                        (Inputs::N_qcd_mu + Inputs::c_mu * (Inputs::N_ttbar_mu + Inputs::N_w_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu))*(1-Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu);
      N_LT_pred_mu = (1-Inputs::eps_sig_mu)*(Inputs::N_ttbar_mu + Inputs::N_w_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu)/Inputs::eps_sig_mu
                     + (1-Inputs::eps_qcd_mu)*Inputs::N_qcd_mu/Inputs::eps_qcd_mu;
*/     

      N_pre_tt_e = Inputs::Luminosity * Inputs::Br_tt_ej * Inputs::Selection_eff_e * x[_nparam-2];
      N_pre_tt_mu = Inputs::Luminosity * Inputs::Br_tt_mj * Inputs::Selection_eff_mu * x[_nparam-2];

      N_plus_pred_e = N_pre_tt_e * (1-Inputs::c_e) * (1 + x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                      (Inputs::N_w_e*Inputs::f_w_p_e + Inputs::N_mc_e * Inputs::f_mc_p_e) * (1-Inputs::c_e) +
                      (Inputs::N_qcd_e + Inputs::c_e * (N_pre_tt_e + Inputs::N_w_e + Inputs::N_mc_e))*Inputs::f_qcd_p_e;
      N_minus_pred_e = N_pre_tt_e * (1-Inputs::c_e) * (1 - x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                       (Inputs::N_w_e*Inputs::f_w_m_e + Inputs::N_mc_e * Inputs::f_mc_m_e) * (1-Inputs::c_e) +
                       (Inputs::N_qcd_e + Inputs::c_e * (N_pre_tt_e + Inputs::N_w_e + Inputs::N_mc_e))*Inputs::f_qcd_m_e;
      N_LT_pred_e = (1-Inputs::eps_sig_e)*(N_pre_tt_e + Inputs::N_w_e + Inputs::N_mc_e)/Inputs::eps_sig_e
                    + (1-Inputs::eps_qcd_e)*Inputs::N_qcd_e/Inputs::eps_qcd_e;

      N_plus_pred_mu = N_pre_tt_mu * (1-Inputs::c_mu) * (1 + x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                       (Inputs::N_w_mu*Inputs::f_w_p_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu * Inputs::f_mc_p_mu) * (1-Inputs::c_mu) +
                       (Inputs::N_qcd_mu + Inputs::c_mu * (N_pre_tt_mu + Inputs::N_w_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu))*Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu;
      N_minus_pred_mu = N_pre_tt_mu * (1-Inputs::c_mu) * (1 - x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                        (Inputs::N_w_mu*Inputs::f_w_m_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu * Inputs::f_mc_m_mu) * (1-Inputs::c_mu) +
                        (Inputs::N_qcd_mu + Inputs::c_mu * (N_pre_tt_mu + Inputs::N_w_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu))*Inputs::f_qcd_m_mu;
      N_LT_pred_mu = (1-Inputs::eps_sig_mu)*(N_pre_tt_mu + Inputs::N_w_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu)/Inputs::eps_sig_mu
                     + (1-Inputs::eps_qcd_mu)*Inputs::N_qcd_mu/Inputs::eps_qcd_mu;

/*    //test
      N_pre_tt_e = Inputs::Luminosity * Inputs::Br_tt_ej * Inputs::Selection_eff_e * x[_nparam-2];
      N_pre_tt_mu = Inputs::Luminosity * Inputs::Br_tt_mj * Inputs::Selection_eff_mu * x[_nparam-2];
      N_plus_pred_e = N_pre_tt_e * (1 + x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                      Inputs::N_w_e*Inputs::f_w_p_e + Inputs::N_mc_e * Inputs::f_mc_p_e +
                      Inputs::N_qcd_e*Inputs::f_qcd_p_e;
      N_minus_pred_e = N_pre_tt_e * (1 - x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                       Inputs::N_w_e*(1-Inputs::f_w_p_e) + Inputs::N_mc_e * (1-Inputs::f_mc_p_e) +
                       Inputs::N_qcd_e*(1-Inputs::f_qcd_p_e);
      N_LT_pred_e = (1-Inputs::eps_qcd_e)*Inputs::N_qcd_e/Inputs::eps_qcd_e;

      N_pre_tt_mu = Inputs::Luminosity * Inputs::Br_tt_mj * Inputs::Selection_eff_mu * x[_nparam-2];
      N_plus_pred_mu = N_pre_tt_mu * (1 + x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                       (Inputs::N_w_mu*Inputs::f_w_p_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu * Inputs::f_mc_p_mu) +
                       Inputs::N_qcd_mu*Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu;
      N_minus_pred_mu = N_pre_tt_mu * (1 - x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                        (Inputs::N_w_mu*(1-Inputs::f_w_p_mu) + Inputs::N_mc_mu * (1-Inputs::f_mc_p_mu)) +
                        Inputs::N_qcd_mu*(1-Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu);
      N_LT_pred_mu = (1-Inputs::eps_qcd_mu)*Inputs::N_qcd_mu/Inputs::eps_qcd_mu;
*/ 
   //============== Compute -Log(lhood) ===================
    //  Minus log likelihood = Minus(sum of ln (gauss(x))  + sum of ln (Poisson))

      loglhood += LogPoissonProb(Inputs::N_plus_obs_e, N_plus_pred_e);
      loglhood += LogPoissonProb(Inputs::N_minus_obs_e, N_minus_pred_e);
      loglhood += LogPoissonProb(Inputs::N_LT_obs_e, N_LT_pred_e);
      //loglhood += LogPoissonProb(x[_nparam-2],N_LT_pred[0]);
 
      loglhood += LogPoissonProb(Inputs::N_plus_obs_mu, N_plus_pred_mu);
      loglhood += LogPoissonProb(Inputs::N_minus_obs_mu, N_minus_pred_mu);
      loglhood += LogPoissonProb(Inputs::N_LT_obs_mu, N_LT_pred_mu);
      //loglhood += LogPoissonProb(x[_nparam-3],N_LT_pred[1]);

   }

   if (setuputil::CHANNEL_TYPE == 1)
   {
/*    ///test
      N_plus_pred_e = Inputs::N_ttbar_e * (1-Inputs::c_e) * (1 + x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                      (Inputs::N_w_e*Inputs::f_w_p_e + Inputs::N_mc_e * Inputs::f_mc_p_e) * (1-Inputs::c_e) +
                      (Inputs::N_qcd_e + Inputs::c_e * (Inputs::N_ttbar_e + Inputs::N_w_e + Inputs::N_mc_e))*Inputs::f_qcd_p_e;
      N_minus_pred_e = Inputs::N_ttbar_e * (1-Inputs::c_e) * (1 - x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                       (Inputs::N_w_e*(1-Inputs::f_w_p_e) + Inputs::N_mc_e * (1-Inputs::f_mc_p_e)) * (1-Inputs::c_e) +
                       (Inputs::N_qcd_e + Inputs::c_e * (Inputs::N_ttbar_e + Inputs::N_w_e + Inputs::N_mc_e))*(1-Inputs::f_qcd_p_e);
      N_LT_pred_e = (1-Inputs::eps_sig_e)*(Inputs::N_ttbar_e + Inputs::N_w_e + Inputs::N_mc_e)/Inputs::eps_sig_e
                    + (1-Inputs::eps_qcd_e)*Inputs::N_qcd_e/Inputs::eps_qcd_e;
*/

      N_pre_tt_e = Inputs::Luminosity * Inputs::Br_tt_ej * Inputs::Selection_eff_e * x[_nparam-2];
      //cout << Inputs::Luminosity << " " << Inputs::Br_tt_ej << " " << Inputs::Selection_eff_e << endl;
      N_plus_pred_e = N_pre_tt_e * (1-Inputs::c_e) * (1 + x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                      (Inputs::N_w_e*Inputs::f_w_p_e + Inputs::N_mc_e * Inputs::f_mc_p_e) * (1-Inputs::c_e) +
                      (Inputs::N_qcd_e + Inputs::c_e * (N_pre_tt_e + Inputs::N_w_e + Inputs::N_mc_e))*Inputs::f_qcd_p_e;
      N_minus_pred_e = N_pre_tt_e * (1-Inputs::c_e) * (1 - x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                       (Inputs::N_w_e*Inputs::f_w_m_e + Inputs::N_mc_e * Inputs::f_mc_m_e) * (1-Inputs::c_e) +
                       (Inputs::N_qcd_e + Inputs::c_e * (N_pre_tt_e + Inputs::N_w_e + Inputs::N_mc_e))*Inputs::f_qcd_m_e;
      N_LT_pred_e = (1-Inputs::eps_sig_e)*(N_pre_tt_e + Inputs::N_w_e + Inputs::N_mc_e)/Inputs::eps_sig_e
                    + (1-Inputs::eps_qcd_e)*Inputs::N_qcd_e/Inputs::eps_qcd_e;
      //cout << N_LT_pred_e << " " << Inputs::N_LT_obs_e << " " << x[_nparam-2] << endl;
      
/*    ///test
      N_pre_tt_e = Inputs::Luminosity * Inputs::Br_tt_ej * Inputs::Selection_eff_e * x[_nparam-2];
      //cout << Inputs::Luminosity << " " << Inputs::Br_tt_ej << " " << Inputs::Selection_eff_e << endl;
      N_plus_pred_e = N_pre_tt_e * (1 + x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                      Inputs::N_w_e*Inputs::f_w_p_e + Inputs::N_mc_e * Inputs::f_mc_p_e +
                      Inputs::N_qcd_e*Inputs::f_qcd_p_e;
      N_minus_pred_e = N_pre_tt_e * (1 - x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                       Inputs::N_w_e*(1-Inputs::f_w_p_e) + Inputs::N_mc_e * (1-Inputs::f_mc_p_e) +
                       Inputs::N_qcd_e*(1-Inputs::f_qcd_p_e);
      N_LT_pred_e = (1-Inputs::eps_qcd_e)*Inputs::N_qcd_e/Inputs::eps_qcd_e;
*/
      loglhood += LogPoissonProb(Inputs::N_plus_obs_e, N_plus_pred_e);
      loglhood += LogPoissonProb(Inputs::N_minus_obs_e, N_minus_pred_e);
      loglhood += LogPoissonProb(Inputs::N_LT_obs_e, N_LT_pred_e);
     // loglhood += LogPoissonProb(Inputs::N_LT_obs_e, x[_nparam-3]);

   }

   if (setuputil::CHANNEL_TYPE == 2)
   {
/*    ///test
      N_plus_pred_mu = Inputs::N_ttbar_mu * (1-Inputs::c_mu) * (1 + x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                       (Inputs::N_w_mu*Inputs::f_w_p_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu * Inputs::f_mc_p_mu) * (1-Inputs::c_mu) +
                       (Inputs::N_qcd_mu + Inputs::c_mu * (Inputs::N_ttbar_mu + Inputs::N_w_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu))*Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu;
      N_minus_pred_mu = Inputs::N_ttbar_mu * (1-Inputs::c_mu) * (1 - x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                        (Inputs::N_w_mu*(1-Inputs::f_w_p_mu) + Inputs::N_mc_mu * (1-Inputs::f_mc_p_mu)) * (1-Inputs::c_mu) +
                        (Inputs::N_qcd_mu + Inputs::c_mu * (Inputs::N_ttbar_mu + Inputs::N_w_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu))*(1-Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu);
      N_LT_pred_mu = (1-Inputs::eps_sig_mu)*(Inputs::N_ttbar_mu + Inputs::N_w_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu)/Inputs::eps_sig_mu
                     + (1-Inputs::eps_qcd_mu)*Inputs::N_qcd_mu/Inputs::eps_qcd_mu;
*/
/*    ///this is for gluon dilution study
      N_plus_pred_mu = Inputs::N_ttbar_mu * (1-Inputs::c_mu) * (1 + f_c * x[_nparam-1] + f_w * x[_nparam-2])/2 +
                       (Inputs::N_w_mu*Inputs::f_w_p_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu * Inputs::f_mc_p_mu) * (1-Inputs::c_mu) +
                       (Inputs::N_qcd_mu + Inputs::c_mu * (Inputs::N_ttbar_mu + Inputs::N_w_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu))*Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu;
      N_minus_pred_mu = Inputs::N_ttbar_mu * (1-Inputs::c_mu) * (1 - f_c * x[_nparam-1] + f_w * x[_nparam-2])/2 +
                        (Inputs::N_w_mu*(1-Inputs::f_w_p_mu) + Inputs::N_mc_mu * (1-Inputs::f_mc_p_mu)) * (1-Inputs::c_mu) +
                        (Inputs::N_qcd_mu + Inputs::c_mu * (Inputs::N_ttbar_mu + Inputs::N_w_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu))*(1-Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu);
*/

      N_pre_tt_mu = Inputs::Luminosity * Inputs::Br_tt_mj * Inputs::Selection_eff_mu * x[_nparam-2];
      N_plus_pred_mu = N_pre_tt_mu * (1-Inputs::c_mu) * (1 + x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                       (Inputs::N_w_mu*Inputs::f_w_p_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu * Inputs::f_mc_p_mu) * (1-Inputs::c_mu) +
                       (Inputs::N_qcd_mu + Inputs::c_mu * (N_pre_tt_mu + Inputs::N_w_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu))*Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu;
      N_minus_pred_mu = N_pre_tt_mu * (1-Inputs::c_mu) * (1 - x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                        (Inputs::N_w_mu*Inputs::f_w_m_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu * Inputs::f_mc_m_mu) * (1-Inputs::c_mu) +
                        (Inputs::N_qcd_mu + Inputs::c_mu * (N_pre_tt_mu + Inputs::N_w_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu))*Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu;
      N_LT_pred_mu = (1-Inputs::eps_sig_mu)*(N_pre_tt_mu + Inputs::N_w_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu)/Inputs::eps_sig_mu
                     + (1-Inputs::eps_qcd_mu)*Inputs::N_qcd_mu/Inputs::eps_qcd_mu;

/*    //test
      N_pre_tt_mu = Inputs::Luminosity * Inputs::Br_tt_mj * Inputs::Selection_eff_mu * x[_nparam-2];
      N_plus_pred_mu = N_pre_tt_mu * (1 + x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                       (Inputs::N_w_mu*Inputs::f_w_p_mu + Inputs::N_mc_mu * Inputs::f_mc_p_mu) +
                       Inputs::N_qcd_mu*Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu;
      N_minus_pred_mu = N_pre_tt_mu * (1 - x[_nparam-1])/2 +
                        (Inputs::N_w_mu*(1-Inputs::f_w_p_mu) + Inputs::N_mc_mu * (1-Inputs::f_mc_p_mu)) +
                        Inputs::N_qcd_mu*(1-Inputs::f_qcd_p_mu);
      N_LT_pred_mu = (1-Inputs::eps_qcd_mu)*Inputs::N_qcd_mu/Inputs::eps_qcd_mu;
*/
      loglhood += LogPoissonProb(Inputs::N_plus_obs_mu, N_plus_pred_mu);
      loglhood += LogPoissonProb(Inputs::N_minus_obs_mu, N_minus_pred_mu);
      loglhood += LogPoissonProb(Inputs::N_LT_obs_mu, N_LT_pred_mu);
   }
    
   //
   f = loglhood;
}


//==============================
//==== poisson probability =====
//==============================
double LogPoissonProb(double Nobserved, double Nexpected)
{
  //  cout << "Nexpected " << Nexpected << endl;
  if(Nexpected<0.0000001) return 100000;
  return Nexpected - Nobserved*log(Nexpected);
}



//---------------------------------------------------
double poisson(double nbar, double n)
//---------------------------------------------------
{
    double u = 1;
    for( int i=0 ; i<n ; i++ ) {
      u *= nbar/(i+1);
    }
    return u*exp(-nbar);
}
